I rarely give five stars, but this place has great food.

I  toying with the idea of going vegan, so I'm looking around for  vegan options. I discover this place. Four out of seven items on their menu are vegetarian, and could become vegan with a couple of special requests.

You won't miss the meat, and they have two chicken options of you insist on that sort of protein.

I hope they are a success and open more restaurants. The only one that stays open for dinner is at Figueroa and 7th. The other two are only open for lunch.<//Text>

<pics>None</pics><text>Indian for the Non-Indian
As a "noob" of Indian cuisine I cannot speak to the authenticity of the food, I can only speak to what it tastes like on my palate.  I basically stick to the Chicken Masala or the Chicken Curry.  Both wonderful dishes on their own and in combination of the garlic naan that they have.  There are pros and cons to the chicken curry though.  The chicken is cooked thru a little better so the chicken is more tender and moist but if you are going into a client meeting in the afternoon, don't eat it for lunch.

Hot and Cool
Be aware, the spicy sauce, drum roll please......is freakin' spicy.  Go figure right? A spicy sauce that is finally spicy.  A little too spicy I may say, but it may be awesome for more manly men than me.  The good thing is, there's also a cool minty sauce to cool down your tongue if you accidently add too much spicy sauce!</text></record>

< Rate>
4</Rate>
< Review>
It was closed the day I visited, but from the other reviews it looks like I didn't miss much. Almost all the exhibits are outside the locked doors and are available to view in the zoology building. Some had information, most just a name. I loved seeing the Tyrannosaurus up close. There were several other skulls and a few other skeletons. Another highlight for me was the cast of Lucy, the hominid found by Dr Leaky and his team that inspired so many people's interest in anthropology. It isn't a very big place, and as interested as I was, I only spent a couple of hours. Several tour groups came through spending more like 10 or 15 minutes. It's a place to visit if you are interested and near the campus, but I wouldn't call it a destination into itself.<//Review>

< Text>
After upgrading to this location I hope to never go back to the other 24 hour fitness gyms! It is attached to the The Shoppes at Carlsbad (mall). The front desk staff always has a smile on his or her face and asks if they can help. Super nice and helpful. Especially Micheal, he has a great smile and customer service! I really appreciate the warm welcomes here from him and others too. My husband and I normally use the jacuzzi and shower. Huge plus there is lockers with complimentary codes you can enter for free for use. (If you don't have your own lock.) The people who come here are really nice too when we enter or exit the jacuzzi or someone is walking by, other members are kind to turn the knob to give jacuzzi more time since it is only in 15 minute intervals. Huge plus with getting super sport membership along with the lockers you get complimentary plastic bags for wet clothes if needed, and a machine to dry your swimsuit in a matter of seconds! Another huge positive is I never ran into any maintenance people! And I'm here normally in the late evening or graveyard times. There are friendly staff, friendly other fellow gym members, clean space and complimentary/convenient items for you! This is a great gym.< /Text>

<user>113878263300592622944< /user>< Review>
Lovely neighborhood space with good coffee.  The morning pastries are mostly good, but occasionally the savory pastries can be greasy, heavy, or poorly seasoned.  Morning buns, cinnamon twists, cream cheese pastries, and cookies are consistently good. Each pastry is about $5.  One thing I like is the variety of options - this is not your typical chain coffee store pastry selection.  The staff is really nice and helpful.  The pizzas are very good - different toppings daily. $3 slice, $24 whole. Closed Mondays and Tuesdays.</Review>

OK, here is a good surprise! I rate La Hacienda 5 of 5 stars. Sometimes the best Mexican restaurants are the little hole-in-the-wall locations. La Hacienda is relatively small with a few patio tables. The shining star is the food and salsa. Perhaps the simplest Mexican menu that I've seen with a hand-full of choices, but, easy to find several favorite choices in the set. The chips and salsa are really enjoyable. The food is outstanding! Yes, I was surprised. It was really good. It took a Groupon to get me to notice this place, but, I assure you that I'll be returning.<//review>

<Review>I love Mongolian bbq and they do the best! You have to fill out a paper if you walk in with what you want, you just go thru and circle what you want as far as type of meat, veggies and how any scoops of the different types of sauces. If you are not sure let them know you want flavor and or if you want it spicy and they are more than happy to help you fill it out. They will hook you up and it is the bomb. The Mongolian bbq is $10.77 out the door, it comes with your choice of chicken fried rice or white rice and a veggie egg roll. Mask is required to enter and they do have plastic up around. They do ask if your ordering any thing else besides Mongolian bbq call the order on ahead of time and pick it up (signs posted). The portions are large and me and my husbands can share and get full!< /Review><pics>None</pics><resp>None<//resp>< gmapID>

<Text>Nothing I like more than a local Mom n Pop family oriented restaurant that serves excellent food! Friendly staff, good service, great food and extremely affordable price.

Been a huge fan of this place for over a decade. They have everything here. Awesome lunch & dinner combos. Chinese Food and Mongolian BBQ. A nice option to pick from.

Let's start with their Mongolian BBQ. I like it hot. Left over eating cold is even better cause it taste better than 15$ a La Bou Salad. For a good sized bowl filled with meat and vegetables, 1.5 scoop of all the dark sauces and 2 full scoops of oil ( combo of sesame and hot.) bowl of  cabbage soup, rice (steamed or fried) and egg rolls comes with it! Cheese wonton with dinner combo. Did I mention they make BEST cream cheese wontons in the world???

Their Chinese food is out of this world. I can't find another place to compare it with. Wor Wonton Soup is super hearty with chicken, beef shrimp loaded with cabbage. A meal within itself. Their Fried Rice and chow mein is un believably tasty. Walnut prawns, is so creamy it melts in your mouth. Chicken wings, cheese wontons, general chicken & triple delight. YUMM! I can't name everything off the menu. But EVERYTHING they make is good!

It's Chinese American Fusion and I am addicted to this place.< /Text>< response>
